< Review>
Firstly, I appreciate the customer service. It was my first time visiting and I didn't feel rushed.
I ordered macaroons, a chai latte, and pre-ordered a straeberry & cream cake! Macarons are delicious and fluffy, and huge! In my opinion. Usually you find them a lot smaller in other bakeries. The latte was yummy, and they also have Vietnamese coffee if you're in search of q place.
As for the cake, it looked delicious, so I hope my eyes are on par with my taste buds.
But really, service is key and I was impressed. Trying to support our small and local businesses üëç<//Review>

< Review>
Cute little Paris bakery cafe in Rancho Cucamonga. It's a family owned and run business. It's adorable from the first step you take in. The sweets are delicious. I got the coconut cake and lime tart. The macroon were soft, definitely get the Nutella one and strawberry. The Earl grey macroon was a little hard. Great tea and coffee selection. Very comfortable seating, great for an afternoon desserts and tea or a late evening relaxation. They have a kids play section too!< /Review>

5<//rating>
<Gmap_id>0x80c335def4b3c8d5:0x695754ba422df9ff< /Gmap_id><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMLHQZvIRQHEdCwcjQeyqNo8yOee3eNIRTNoB-9=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMbjtFBDkMznH_pIx64WUiORSPE0WR71Ew0FcH3=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPMPF39xcvaBtWqGdNBX41_f9FrrkqExKq0tr92=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPVSojphE3fMqjouyXWqFhOnnWW65vuGvAKiK9H=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</Pics><UserId.>110081104878298477501</UserId.></record></dataset><record>
<Review>I've been to Paris maybe 3-4 times, usually in the late afternoon. I would recommend coming earlier as most items are already sold out by evening. Only that first evening was I able to snag most of my goodies - ever since that first visit, most of the cakes were already gone by the time I arrived. Prices are also fair for the quality of desserts and pastries. If you order more than 2-3 items of the same variety, you actually get a discount. And if you mix and match between the mini cakes, you can score 3 for $5.

My favorite item that I've tried has got to be the Palmier. It's $3.50 for one, but the size is humongous - bigger than my head (I have a picture for proof!) and even after a few days, the dessert was still as crispy and sweet as ever. Loved that the outer edges were crispy and sweet, but the inner layers were more soft and flaky.

Almond croissant/almond chocolate croissant at $3.99 each - I didn't get to eat the croissants the same day, but after popping it into the toaster oven, the croissant was still flaky and delicious. I prefer the almond with almond paste inside, but the chocolate wasn't too bad either. I do think that the croissant could have a little more almond paste and be a little sweeter - not my favorite almond croissant, but I would get these again. I've also tried the bread pudding ($3.99), which I feel is a little bit on the pricier side. I saw a lot of raving reviews, and I do think it's tasty but not as flavorful or sweet as I would have preferred. My friend isn't a big fan of super sweet desserts, so he thought this was perfect.

As for the cakes - my favorite is the wedding cake ($4.99 for each slice of cake). Kind of reminded me of the berries and cream cake from Porto's, but instead of berries, this one only had strawberries. The cake was a little melted by the time we dug into it - but the flavor was still there. The cream on the outside was creamy yet lightly whipped while the inside, the strawberries were mixed with a sweet pudding almost. And the cake was light and airy, making for a very delicious bite.

The tiramisu and fraisier cakes were also tasty - I liked the tiramisu a little more because the taste was heavier and richer, but the fraisier resembled a soft cheesecake almost because of the texture. It was super light and not too sweet; can probably eat an entire slice without even realizing it. Black forest was probably our least favorite - not a big fan of the cherries inside, but taste was - again - not sweet and had a good chocolate flavor.

And on another visit, I got the opalys - an almond mousse and raspberry filling inside of an orb. Price was around $5-6, but the dessert is so beautiful and captivating that I didn't mind paying that price to be able to try the flavors. This was a light mousse that had a hint of almond flavor to give the dessert some sweetness, but the added acidity from the raspberry made it perfect. I wouldn't mind ordering another one of these - or trying other flavors of the special orbs that they make.

Don't forget the macarons! One is $2.99, but if you buy more, the prices get cheaper. I bought several for my friend one night, but came back and tried a caramel flavor for myself. Not sure how often these macarons are replenished, but they seem to always have an assortment of flavors in stock. The shell is more chewy than crumbly, but the flavor of that caramel was so tasty and rich, that I didn't mind the kick of sweetness. Getting into the middle of the macaron, it definitely had a chewiness that I enjoyed. Price is a little high, but the size of the macaron is pretty good.

tl;dr - Will be returning as often as I can. Highly recommend the cakes and palmier as well as their special dessert items. The people helping us were are all super friendly and helpful. D√©cor of the place is extremely cute - too bad there isn't any indoor seating. Can definitely go crazy with all my photos if I was able to enjoy my desserts inside.</Review>< user_id>

<text>In terms of their cakes, breads, and foods, they are awesome.

However, in terms of their service, they are seriously terrible.

Today, I went there to purchase a whole cake that has a price tag of about $26-$27. (I had purchased the same cake before and was aware of the price.)

However, when I was paying for the cake, they said it's over $40.
They mentioned that it is the same cake but in larger size.

Because I chose that cake based both on my previous experience AND the price, I said whether they can offer any discount from putting an incorrect price tag.
After a short period, they mentioned that the chef would not want to give any discount.
Because I really liked the cake, I paid the full price.

Then, another staff came out from inside and started to explain that the price tag I saw was for a smaller size (however, there was no smaller size cake(s) of the same kind. The cake I chose was the only one on display) and she also told me that she can show me the difference in sizes.
(She said the cake I chose today was an 8-pieces cake, while the one I had purchased previous was a 6-pieces cake)

Well, since customers do not usually notice whether a cake is 8-pieces or 6-pieces when there is nothing to compare, I said that they should have put the correct price tag instead of trying to justifying themselves.
She didn't apologize and kept teaching me about the difference in size.
I felt that she thinks it's my mistake of incorrectly guessing the size of a cake (with an incorrect price-tag attached) and not their mistake of not putting a correct price-tag.

If she had apologized, then I would have fully understood and purchased the cake.
However, because she started with justification and kept teaching me instead, I finally cancelled the purchase.

By the way, the other staff who was there at first (not the one who came out later and tried to teach me) was polite.

Even if their bakery items and food are great, if their service is not changing, then I think they will lose customers eventually.
They seriously need to educate their staffs first.</text>< Pics>

< Review>
We stopped by here in our way to K Towne 88 to get some coffee and were delighted by all of the pastries and offerings here.

Decor

This place has a cute Parisian theme with indoor and outdoor seating. The facility is clean and gives off a family vibe.

Food

I ordered the bread pudding and a caramel blended drink and my wife ordered a tarte fruit. The tarte fruit was subtly sweet and the fruit was fresh. The bread pudding was thick and moist. I suffered a brain freeze from the caramel blended drink. Drink it slowly since it's very cold but very good.

Verdict

If you're in the area and craving sweets, Paris pastries is an excellent choice for tasty treats.</Review>

< Review>
My girlfriend and I were in the market for mountain bikes. We did a lot of research on local bike stores, selection, etc. and had decided to try out Pure Ride Cycles.

I had actually come to this place back in the 90s and bought a bike! This place is AWESOME! Clean and organized store, large selection, competitive pricing (Smokin' deals!), and most important, SUPERB service!

We had the pleasure of working with Shawn, Trevor and Kristen. They were very knowledgeable, friendly, and made us feel welcomed. I would highly recommend this place to anyone looking to get into or get back into biking! We'll definitely be coming back. Thank you Pure Ride Cycles, you guys ROCK! #NEWBIKEDAY< /Review>

<resp>None< /resp>< Review>
An old Korean restaurant has to compete with newer ones so if you can't beat fresh new fusion by price, decor, or service then you'll be in trouble.

The problem with this is the event is run inefficient and poorly.  Normally places charge by the person but here they charge by plate used. Really odd considering guest don't know that so some guest grab two plates or a new plate for seconds.

The portions provided do not come close to estimates and they always run short on the meats.

DIY. Bad business practice and skimps on meats for events.</Review>

Great little hands-on museum for younger children. Lots of hands-on activities including a kid sized grocery store and kitchen. A nursery area features lifelike dollies. A flowing flume and water table for exploring water. A Tot Spot allow under 3 visitor their own place to explore. Puzzles, a puppet theater and lots of interesting things to explore and learn. <pictures>None< /pictures><resp>None< /resp><GmapID>0x54d1557b2d9f48c7:0x938a3dc0b6f00764</GmapID></record></dataset><record>
< UserId.>
117587048614180214902</UserId.>
<username>Ryann Pinnegar<//username><time>1518261094485< /time><Rating>5<//Rating>< Text>
This is a great place to take kids. Every activity provides an opportunity for children to explore and engage their brains and their bodies. The activities are hands on and easy to learn how to do. There is an awesome pretend play area with a grocery store area and a kitchen area. There is a book nook, easy access to family restrooms, and friendly staff. I would say Redwood Discovery Museum is geared toward kids younger than 10, but teens and adults can also enjoy trying out many of the activities. This is an ideal place to hang out on rainy and cold days when you can't take tge kids to the park. The museum often hosts free play groups, which is a great way to try it out for free. But the play group is very popular, so the museum can get crowded. It is well worth the cost of admission (or a membership) to visit when there isn't crowd. A tip for those who are easily over-stimulated by noise: take ear plugs, especially if you are going during a time when there are lots of other visitors.</Text>
